when you say she's a programmer , she did do some , but the real thing is to have said the future is going to be much , much more than this .	當你說她是個計劃師 , 她做了一些 , 但真正的重點是 , 未來要有更多 。
now , a hundred years later , this guy comes along , alan turing , and in 1936 , and invents the computer all over again .	現在 , 一百年後 , 這個傢伙來到1936年 , 發明了電腦 。
now , of course , babbage's machine was entirely mechanical .	當然 , babbage是一個機械的機械 。
turing's machine was entirely theoretical .	turing是完全合理的 。
both of these guys were coming from a mathematical perspective , but turing told us something very important .	這些傢伙從數學角度來看 , 但要告訴我們一件非常重要的事 。
he laid down the mathematical foundations for computer science , and said , " it doesn't matter how you make a computer . "	他缺乏數學基礎基礎基礎基礎基礎 , 說: 「 它不管你如何製造電腦 」
it doesn't matter if your computer's mechanical , like babbage's was , or electronic , like computers are today , or perhaps in the future , cells , or , again , mechanical again , once we get into nanotechnology .	不管你電腦的機械 , 比如巴比的機械 , 如今電腦一樣 , 或電子 , 或許在未來 , 或在未來 , 再次 , 再次我們進入奈米學 。
we could go back to babbage's machine and just make it tiny . all those things are computers .	我們可以回到babbage的機器 , 只是讓它微小 。 所有這些東西都是電腦 。
there is in a sense a computing essence .	在某種意義上 , 有一個計算機 。
this is called the church–turing thesis .	這叫做教堂教堂 ,
and so suddenly , you get this link where you say this thing babbage had built really was a computer .	突然間 , 你就得到了這張圖書館 , 你說這個東西babbage建造真的是個電腦 。
in fact , it was capable of doing everything we do today with computers , only really slowly .	事實上 , 我們今天能用電腦來做所有事情 , 都很慢 。
to give you an idea of how slowly , it had about 1k of memory .	為了給各位一個想法如何慢地 , 它有大約一公里 。
it used punch cards , which were being fed in , and it ran about 10 , 000 times slower the first zx81 .	它用了一萬倍的車子 , 它被餵飽了大約一萬倍 。
it did have a ram pack .	它有一個罕見的原型 。
you could add on a lot of extra memory if you wanted to .	你可以在很多外交記憶中加上很多 。
so , where does that bring us today ?	那麼 , 這帶給我們什麼樣子 ?
so there are plans .	所以有計劃 。
over in swindon , the science museum archives , there are hundreds of plans and thousands of pages of notes written by charles babbage about this analytical engine .	在瑞典博物館裡 , 科學博物館裡有數百種植物和數千個非寫作 , 關於這種分析工程程程程 。
one of those is a set of plans that we call plan 28 , and that is also the name of a charity that i started with doron swade , who was the curator of computing at the science museum , and also the person who drove the project to build a difference engine , and our plan is to build it .	其中之一就是我們所謂的計劃之一 , 這也是我所謂的慈善機構 , 他是來自科學博物館 , 他是從科學博物館的曲線 , 而我們的計畫就是建造一個不同的工程師 , 我們的計畫就是建造它 。
here in south kensington , we will build the analytical engine .	在南韓 , 我們會建構一個分析工程程 。
the project has a number of parts to it .	這項計畫有數量的部分 。
one was the scanning of babbage's archive .	第一是巴bbage的掃描 。
that's been done . the second is now the study of all of those plans to determine what to build .	第二個計畫已經完成了 。 現在第二個計畫來決定建造什麼 。
the third part is a computer simulation of that machine , and the last part is to physically build it at the science museum .	第三個部分是電腦模擬電腦模擬博物館 , 最後一部分是物理博物館 。
when it's built , you'll finally be able to understand how a computer works , because rather than having a tiny chip in front of you , you've got to look at this humongous thing and say , " ah , i see the memory operating , i see the cpu operating , i hear it operating . i probably smell it operating . "	當它建構時 , 你終於可以理解電腦運作 , 因為不是有小小的晶片 , 而是在你面前 , 你必須仔細觀察這個奇怪的事情 , 然後說: 「 嗯 , 我看到了記憶體 」 。
but in between that we're going to do a simulation .	但在此時 , 我們要做一個模擬 。
babbage himself wrote , he said , as soon as the analytical engine exists , it will surely guide the future course of science .	babbage寫著 , 他說 , 身為分析工程程存在 , 它會確保科學的未來 。
of course , he never built it , because he was always fiddling with new plans , but when it did get built , of course , in the 1940s , everything changed .	當然 , 他從來沒有建構它 , 因為他總是用新的計劃 , 但在1940年代 , 一切都改變了 。
now , i'll just give you a little taste of what it looks like in motion with a video which shows just one part of the cpu mechanism working .	現在 , 我要給各位一點一點一點一點點 , 它看起來像在動機體運作的其中一部分之一 , 顯示一部分乾淨機制之一 。
so this is just three sets of cogs , and it's going to add . this is the adding mechanism in action , so you imagine this gigantic machine .	所以這只是三組認知機制 , 它將會加上行動機制 , 所以你想像這台巨大的機制 , 所以你想像一下這個巨大機器 。
so , give me five years .	所以 , 給我五年了 。
before the 2030s happen , we'll have it .	在2030年發生之前 , 我們會得到 。
thank you very much .	非常謝謝各位 。

in this accessible talk from tedxboston , richard resnick shows how cheap and fast genome sequencing is about to turn health care upside down .	在tedxboton的演講中 , 理查尼克•尼克•尼克•尼克•尼克•尼克•安德雷克說: 「 健康照護 」 。
dna , biotech , health care , science , technology	dna、健康照護、科學、科學、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、技術、
richard resnick: welcome to the genomic revolution	理查•尼克:歡迎到基因革命 。
ladies and gentlemen , i present to you the human genome .	女士們 , 我向各位展示人類基因組 。
chromosome one , top left .	染色體第一 , 左邊 。
bottom right are the sex chromosomes .	底部是性染色體染色體 。
women have two copies of that big x chromosome ; men have the x and , of course , that small copy of the y .	婦女有兩個複製基因組 , 當然 , 男人有x和x , 當然 , 那個小的複製 。
sorry boys , but it's just a tiny little thing that makes you different .	抱歉男孩 , 但這只是個小東西讓你不同 。
so if you zoom in on this genome , then what you see , of course , is this double helix structure the code of life spelled out with these four biochemical letters , or we call them bases , right: a , c , g and t .	所以 , 如果你在這個基因組中 , 你會看到的 , 當然 , 這是這雙雙胞胎結構的編碼碼碼碼碼碼碼碼碼 , 或者我們稱它們為蝙蝠 , 或者我們稱它們為蝙蝠 , 等等 。

about 200 times usually .	大約有200倍 。

so i did a few prototypes . i got a small little grant at stanford .	所以我做了幾張照片 , 我拿了一小塊小塊 ,

in the last decade there's been an explosion of use of bone marrow stem cells to treat the patient's other diseases such as heart disease , vascular disease , orthopedics , tissue engineering , even in neurology to treat parkinson's and diabetes .	在過去十年間 , 有一大堆骨幹細胞 , 來治療病人的其他疾病 , 例如心臟疾病 , 或藥物 , 甚至在神經元中 , 甚至在神經元上治療公園 , 甚至在神經元中 。

the hope is that this gets more stem cells out , which translates to better outcomes .	希望的是 , 這個希望讓更多幹細胞更好的結果 , 轉換成更好的結果 。

physicist and surfer garrett lisi presents a controversial new model of the universe that just maybe answers all the big questions . if nothing else , it's the most beautiful 8dimensional model of elementary particles and forces you've ever seen .	物理學家和urfergarretlitsssetlis和urfergarret的宇宙模型 , 可能回答所有大問題 。 如果沒有什麼 , 它是最美麗的8度 。
physics , science , technology	物理、科學、科學、科技、科技、技術 。
garrett lisi on his theory of everything	伽利略在他的理論上 。
whoa , dude . check out those killer equations . sweet .	哇 , 哇 ! 看看那些殺人方程式 。 瑞典 。
actually , for the next 18 minutes i'm going to do the best i can to describe the beauty of particle physics without equations .	事實上 , 接下來的18分鐘我要做最好的 , 我可以描述粒子物理大象物理學的美麗 。
it turns out there's a lot we can learn from coral .	結果發現 , 有很多我們可以從珊瑚身上學到的 。
coral is a very beautiful and unusual animal .	珊瑚是非常美麗的動物 。
each coral head consists of thousand of individual polyps .	每個珊瑚頭頭部都有數千個個人的頭部 。
these polyps are continually budding and branching into genetically identical neighbors .	這些可能是持續虐待和鳥類的鄰居 , 將基因移植到基因上 。
if we imagine this to be a hyperintelligent coral , we can single out an individual and ask him a reasonable question .	如果我們想像一下這是個超級的珊瑚 , 我們可以單單獨的角度 , 問他一個有理由的問題來問他一個理由的問題 。
we can ask how exactly he got to be in this particular location compared to his neighbors if it was just chance , or destiny , or what ?	我們可以問他如何在這個特定的鄰居 , 如果它只是機會 , 或慾望 , 或慾望 , 或否則呢 ?
now , after admonishing us for turning the temperature up too high , he would tell us that our question was completely stupid .	現在 , 在一個月後使用溫度太高了 , 他會告訴我們 , 我們的問題是完全愚蠢 。
these corals can be quite kind of mean , you see , and i have surfing scars to prove that .	這些珊瑚可能很像 , 你看到 , 我有驚訝 , 為了證明這一點 。
but this polyp would continue and tell us that his neighbors were quite clearly identical copies of him .	但這可能持續 , 告訴我們 , 他的鄰居很明顯地 , 他的鄰居很明顯地 。
that he was in all these other locations as well , but experiencing them as separate individuals .	他也在這些其他地方的失敗 , 但擴展了他們身為分分分分離 。
for a coral , branching into different copies is the most natural thing in the world .	對珊瑚而言 , 鳥類在世界中最自然的事情是最自然的事情 。
unlike us , a hyperintelligent coral would be uniquely prepared to understand quantum mechanics .	不像我們一樣 , 一個高度的珊瑚可能會很獨特地準備好了解量量量子機械 。
the mathematics of quantum mechanics very accurately describes how our universe works .	量子機械機械非常精確地描述我們的宇宙如何運作 。
and it tells us our reality is continually branching into different possibilities , just like a coral .	它告訴我們我們我們的現實是完全怪異的可能性 , 就像珊瑚一樣 。
it's a weird thing for us humans to wrap our minds around , since we only ever get to experience one possibility .	這是個很奇怪的事 , 因為我們只能經歷我們的腦袋 , 因為我們只能經歷一個可能性 。
this quantum weirdness was first described by erwin schrödinger and his cat .	這種量子奇怪是第一次描述者 , 他的貓咪和他的貓貓 。
the cat likes this version better .	像這個版本更好 。
in this setup , schrödinger is in a box with a radioactive sample that , by the laws of quantum mechanics , branches into a state in which it is radiated and a state in which it is not .	在這個組合中 , chrddinger是盒子裡的一個盒子 , 由量子機械法律、鳥類、鳥類、鳥類的法律 , 不是 。
in the branch in which the sample radiates , it sets off a trigger that releases poison and schrödinger is dead .	在這個樣本中 , 它在沙漠中 , 它讓釋放出一個蛋白質和chrddinger是死的 。
but in the other branch of reality , he remains alive .	但在現實中 , 他仍然活著著 。
these realities are experienced separately by each individual .	這些真實性都被彼此分離 。
as far as either can tell , the other one doesn't exist .	隨著either可以告訴你 , 另一種不存在 。
this seems weird to us , because each of us only experiences an individual existence , and we don't get to see other branches .	這似乎很奇怪 , 因為每個人只經歷一個個人存在的存在 , 而我們卻無法看見其他鳥類 。
it's as if each of us , like schrödinger here , are a kind of coral branching into different possibilities .	如同我們每一個人一樣 , 像是chrddingerdinger , 有點像珊瑚鳥一樣 。
the mathematics of quantum mechanics tells us this is how the world works at tiny scales .	量子機械機械告訴我們這是怎麼運作的 。
it can be summed up in a single sentence: everything that can happen , does .	它可以在單一句句句句子裡的一切都有可能發生 。
but this does not mean everything happens .	但這並不代表一切發生 。
the rest of physics is about describing what can happen and what can't .	物理學的其他部分是關於描述什麼可能發生什麼事 , 且無法做到 。
what physics tells us is that everything comes down to geometry and the interactions of elementary particles .	物理學告訴我們 , 一切都會下下下降到幾何原子粒子和互動的互動 。
and things can happen only if these interactions are perfectly balanced .	如果這些互動是不可能的平衡是平衡的 。
now i'll go ahead and describe how we know about these particles , what they are and how this balance works .	現在我會走進一步 , 描述我們如何了解這些粒子的運作方式 , 它們是如何運作的 。
in this machine , a beam of protons and antiprotons are accelerated to near the speed of light and brought together in a collision , producing a burst of pure energy .	在這個機器中 , 有一塊蛋白質和螞蟻的速度 , 將近光放到光線的速度 , 促進一個冷靜的能量 。
this energy is immediately converted into a spray of subatomic particles , with detectors and computers used to figure out their properties .	這能量是馬上轉化成一個小粒子的粒子 , 有偵測器和電腦一樣 , 用來找出他們的特性粒子 。
this enormous machine the large hadron collider at cern in geneva has a circumference of 17 miles and , when it's operating , draws five times as much power as the city of monterey .	這個龐大的機器中 , 大型的鐵路上有17英哩 , 當它正在操作時 , 畫出五倍 , 畫出五倍 。
we can't predict specifically what particles will be produced in any individual collision .	我們無法預測特定的粒子會在任何個體中產生的粒子 。
quantum mechanics tells us all possibilities are realized .	量子機械告訴我們所有可能的可能性 。
but physics does tell us what particles can be produced .	但物理學會告訴我們粒子有什麼粒子 。
these particles must have just as much mass and energy as is carried in by the proton and antiproton .	這些粒子一定只是質量和能量被釋放出來 。
any particles more massive than this energy limit aren't produced , and remain invisible to us .	任何粒子的粒子比這個能量更大 , 而永續發展不可思議 。
this is why this new particle accelerator is so exciting .	這就是為什麼這個新粒子的新粒子是非常興奮的 。
it's going to push this energy limit seven times beyond what's ever been done before , so we're going to get to see some new particles very soon .	要把這個能量推進這個能量限制的7倍 , 所以我們將會看到一些新粒子非常快 。
but before talking about what we might see , let me describe the particles we already know of .	但在談論我們所看到的 , 讓我描述我們已經知道的粒子 。
there's a whole zoo of subatomic particles .	有一整體粒子粒子粒子 。
most of us are familiar with electrons .	我們大多數人都熟悉電子 。
a lot of people in this room make a good living pushing them around .	在這個房間裡有很多人 , 讓他們圍繞著他們身邊 。
but the electron also has a neutral partner called the neutrino , with no electric charge and a very tiny mass .	但電子也有一個中央夥伴叫做 「 營養者 」 , 沒有電荷和一個非常微小的質量 。
in contrast , the upanddown quarks have very large masses , and combine in threes to make the protons and neutrons inside atoms .	在矛盾中 , 最大的大量量量 , 三種可以讓原子子子子子子和中間的組合 。
all of these matter particles come in left and righthanded varieties , and have antiparticle partners that carry opposite charges .	所有這些物質粒子都來自左邊和右邊的各種物質 , 而有抗生素合作夥伴 。
these familiar particles also have less familiar second and third generations , which have the same charges as the first but have much higher masses .	這些熟悉粒子粒子粒子也較少熟悉的第二代 , 它有同樣的椅子 。
these matter particles all interact with the various force particles .	這些物質粒子都與各種不同的粒子互動 。
the electromagnetic force interacts with electrically charged matter via particles called photons .	電磁力和電磁力互動互動 , 叫做 「 光子 」 的粒子 」 的粒子 。
there is also a very weak force called , rather unimaginatively , the weak force , that interacts only with lefthanded matter .	有個非常震撼的力量 , 而不是想像力的 , 而是弱勢 , 而是左撇子只有左撇子的作用 。
the strong force acts between quarks which carry a different kind of charge , called color charge , and come in three different varieties: red , green and blue .	夸克之間的強大力量 , 帶著不同的椅子 , 叫做顏色、綠色、綠色、綠色、藍色、藍色、藍色、藍色、藍色 。
you can blame murray gellmann for these names they're his fault .	你可以為這些名字 , 為這些名字 , 他們是他的錯的 。
finally , there's the force of gravity , which interacts with matter via its mass and spin .	最後 , 有重力的力量 , 它與視覺互動 。
the most important thing to understand here is that there's a different kind of charge associated with each of these forces .	最重要的是 , 了解到這裡有一個不同的椅子 , 與這些力量之間的關係 。
these four different forces interact with matter according to the corresponding charges that each particle has .	這四種不同的力量與重要性交互作用 , 每一粒粒粒粒子都有反應 。
a particle that hasn't been seen yet , but we're pretty sure exists , is the higgs particle , which gives masses to all these other particles .	一個粒子沒有看過 , 但我們很確定存在 , 就是暗示粒子粒子粒子粒子粒子 。
the main purpose of the large hadron collider is to see this higgs particle , and we're almost certain it will .	大型的原則是要看到這個希格斯粒子粒子 , 我們幾乎確定它會發生 。
but the greatest mystery is what else we might see .	但最棒的謎題是其他我們所看到的 。
and i'm going to show you one beautiful possibility towards the end of this talk .	我要給各位看一個美麗的可能性 , 向大家展示一個美麗的可能性 。
now , if we count up all these different particles using their various spins and charges , there are 226 .	如果我們把這些不同的粒子和椅子使用不同的粒子和椅子 , 有226 。
that's a lot of particles to keep track of .	這是很多粒子可以繼續追蹤 。
and it seems strange that nature would have so many elementary particles .	它似乎很奇怪的粒子會有很多元素 。
but if we plot them out according to their charges , some beautiful patterns emerge .	但如果我們把它們放到他們的椅子上 , 有些美麗的模式 , 有些美麗的模式 。
the most familiar charge is electric charge .	最熟悉的椅子是電荷的 。
electrons have an electric charge , a negative one , and quarks have electric charges in thirds .	電子有電荷有一個電荷 , 一個負面的負面電荷 , 第三個區域有電荷 。
so when two up quarks and a down quark are combined to make a proton , it has a total electric charge of plus one .	所以 , 當兩個上方公尺時 , 就會被組成一個蛋白質的電荷 , 它必須要有電力的電荷 。
these particles also have antiparticles , which have opposite charges .	這些粒子也有抗生素 , 這種粒子有相反的 。
now , it turns out the electric charge is actually a combination of two other charges: hypercharge and weak charge .	現在 , 結果發現電鏈是兩種其他椅子:hypercharge和弱點 。
if we spread out the hypercharge and weak charge and plot the charges of particles in this twodimensional charge space , the electric charge is where these particles sit along the vertical direction .	如果我們把hypercharge和弱弱弱弱勢 , 把粒子放在兩度空間中 , 電荷空間中 , 電動鏈的電路 , 電荷是這些粒子在垂直方向 。
the electromagnetic and weak forces interact with matter according to their hypercharge and weak charge , which make this pattern .	電磁共振性和弱弱勢互動 , 和震動互動 , 讓這個模式變得更加容易 。
this is called the unified electroweak model , and it was put together back in 1967 .	這是叫做 「 無知的模型 」 模型 , 把它放在1967年 。
the reason most of us are only familiar with electric charge and not both of these is because of the higgs particle .	我們大多數人都只熟悉電鏈的原因 , 而不是兩者都是因為卵子粒子粒子粒子 。
the higgs , over here on the left , has a large mass and breaks the symmetry of this electroweak pattern .	這裡的希格斯 , 在左邊 , 有一個很大的和突破模式的對稱 。
it makes the weak force very weak by giving the weak particles a large mass .	它讓弱勢力變得很弱 , 讓粒子更大 。
since this massive higgs sits along the horizontal direction in this diagram , the photons of electromagnetism remain massless and interact with electric charge along the vertical direction in this charge space .	從這個角度來看 , 在這個圖片中 , 由電磁共振造影 , 電磁共振的光子 , 和電荷的光子相互作用 。
so the electromagnetic and weak forces are described by this pattern of particle charges in twodimensional space .	所以電磁性和弱弱勢力被描述出來 , 在兩度空間中 , 兩度空間的形式 。
we can include the strong force by spreading out its two charge directions and plotting the charges of the force particles in quarks along these directions .	我們可以藉由傳播出來 , 藉由傳播出來的力量 , 將粒子轉換為粒子粒子的力量 。
the charges of all known particles can be plotted in a fourdimensional charge space , and projected down to two dimensions like this so we can see them .	所有人都知道粒子可以在四度空間中被淹沒在四度空間中 , 把它們放到兩維空間 , 像這樣我們可以看見它們 。
whenever particles interact , nature keeps things in a perfect balance along all four of these charge directions .	然而 , 當粒子互動時 , 自然自然持續在完美平衡中 , 四個這些椅子的方向 。
if a particle and an antiparticle collide , it creates a burst of energy and a total charge of zero in all four charge directions .	如果粒子和一個抗體的粒子 , 它會創造出一塊能量 , 它創造出一塊能量 , 每四個椅子的方向 。
at this point , anything can be created as long as it has the same energy and maintains a total charge of zero .	在這一刻 , 任何東西都能創造出一樣的能量和維持一座能量和維持在一起 。
for example , this weak force particle and its antiparticle can be created in a collision .	舉例來說 , 這個弱勢粒子可以在一個冷漠中創造出來的粒子 。
in further interactions , the charges must always balance .	在更進一步的互動中 , 椅子總是平衡 。
one of the weak particles could decay into an electron and an antineutrino , and these three still add to zero total charge .	粒子能偵測到一個電子 , 可以偵測到電子和一個螞蟻 , 而這三仍然加上了零件 。
nature always keeps a perfect balance .	大自然總是保持完美的平衡 。
so these patterns of charges are not just pretty .	所以這些椅子不僅是很棒的 。
they tell us what interactions are allowed to happen .	他們告訴我們互動的互動是如何發生的 。
and we can rotate this charge space in four dimensions to get a better look at the strong interaction , which has this nice hexagonal symmetry .	我們不能把這個椅子放在四度空間中 , 讓一個更好的互動 , 看看強壯的互動 , 這對稱是對稱性對稱 。
in a strong interaction , a strong force particle , such as this one , interacts with a colored quark , such as this green one , to give a quark with a different color charge this red one .	在一個強大的互動中 , 一個強大的粒子 , 比如這個綠色的平方形 , 比如這個綠色的 , 給一個平方形 , 給一個不同的顏色 。
and strong interactions are happening millions of times each second in every atom of our bodies , holding the atomic nuclei together .	每秒鐘都發生了數百萬次 , 每秒鐘都在核子核子核子核能 。
but these four charges corresponding to three forces are not the end of the story .	但這四個慈善家企業家的負責不是故事結束 。
we can also include two more charges corresponding to the gravitational force .	我們也能包含兩種慈善機構的責任 。
when we include these , each matter particle has two different spin charges , spinup and spindown .	當我們加入這些時 , 每一個粒子都有兩個不同的蜘蛛 , 脊髓和脊髓 。
so they all split , and give a nice pattern in sixdimensional charge space .	所以他們都在拼字空間中 , 給一個很好的模式 。
we can rotate this pattern in six dimensions , and see that it's quite pretty .	我們不能把這個模式放在六度空間中 , 看看它很棒 。
right now , this pattern matches our best current knowledge of how nature is built at the tiny scales of these elementary particles .	現在 , 這個模式將我們的最佳知識化的知識是如何在這些元素中建立在微小的粒子 。
this is what we know for certain .	這是我們所知的 。
some of these particles are at the very limit of what we've been able to reach with experiments .	有些粒子在我們身上的一些粒子是可以和實驗的 。
from this pattern , we already know the particle physics of these tiny scales . the way the universe works with these tiny scales is very beautiful .	從這個模式來看 , 我們已經知道粒子物理大小的尺寸 。
but now i'm going to discuss some new and old ideas about things we don't know yet .	但現在我要討論一些新的和舊想法有關我們不知道的東西 。
we want to expand this pattern using mathematics alone , and see if we can get our hands on the whole enchilada .	我們想要擴展這個模式 , 用數學來解釋這個模式 , 如果我們能把手放在整個enanda 。
we want to find all the particles and forces that make a complete picture of our universe .	我們想要找到所有粒子和力量 , 讓宇宙完全相似的圖像 。
and we want to use this picture to predict new particles that we'll see when experiments reach higher energies .	我們想要用這張照片來預測新粒子的新粒子 。
so there's an old idea in particle physics that this known pattern of charges , which is not very symmetric , could emerge from a more perfect pattern that gets broken similar to how the higgs particle breaks the electroweak pattern to give electromagnetism .	所以 , 粒子物理學中有一個古老的想法 , 這不是非常合理的形式 , 而是可以從更完美的形式 , 可以從一個更完美的模式 , 可以從更完美的形式 。
in order to do this , we need to introduce new forces with new charge directions .	為了做到這一點 , 我們需要引導新的領導力 。
when we introduce a new direction , we get to guess what charges the particles have along this direction , and then we can rotate it in with the others .	當我們介紹一個新的方向時 , 我們就能猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜錯
if we guess wisely , we can construct the standard charges in six charge dimensions as a broken symmetry of this more perfect pattern in seven charge dimensions .	如果我們猜想 , 我們就能建構標準標準的標準 , 六個椅子 , 作為一個破碎的對稱 。
this particular choice corresponds to a grand unified theory introduced by pati and salam in 1973 .	這種特殊的珊瑚反應是1973年的理論 , 由pati和alamamamames 。
when we look at this new unified pattern , we can see a couple of gaps where particles seem to be missing .	當我們觀察這個新的統計模式時 , 我們可以看到粒子的差距似乎失敗了 。
this is the way theories of unification work .	這是不可思議的工作的方式 。
a physicist looks for larger , more symmetric patterns that include the established pattern as a subset .	一個物理學家看起來很大 , 更多的對稱 , 包括 「 物質 」 的模式 」 的模式 。
the larger pattern allows us to predict the existence of particles that have never been seen .	最大的模式讓我們預測粒子存在於粒子的存在 。
this unification model predicts the existence of these two new force particles , which should act a lot like the weak force , only weaker .	這個單位模型預測出這兩個新粒子的存在 , 這應該是像弱勢一樣的弱勢 , 只有弱點 。
now we can rotate this set of charges in seven dimensions and consider an odd fact about the matter particles: the second and third generations of matter have exactly the same charges in sixdimensional charge space as the first generation .	現在 , 我們不能把這個椅子放在七度空間中 , 考慮粒子:第二、第三代、第三代的重要性:第二代、第三代的重要性 。
these particles are not uniquely identified by their six charges .	這些粒子不是獨特地辨識到六個椅子 。
they sit on top of one another in the standard charge space .	他們坐在標準的另一端 , 站在標準空間中 。
however , if we work in eightdimensional charge space , then we can assign unique new charges to each particle .	然而 , 如果我們在八度空間中工作 , 那麼我們可以忽略獨特的新規則 , 讓每個粒子獨特的新椅子 。
then we can spin these in eight dimensions , and see what the whole pattern looks like .	然後我們可以在八度內這些圖案中 , 看看整個模式是什麼樣子 。
here we can see the second and third generations of matter now related to the first generation by a symmetry called " triality . "	我們現在可以看到第二代 , 第三代的重要世代 , 叫做 「 三世代 」 。
this particular pattern of charges in eight dimensions is actually part of the most beautiful geometric structure in mathematics .	在八度中 , 這種特殊模式中 , 實際上是數學最美麗的結構 。
it's a pattern of the largest exceptional lie group , e8 .	這是一群最大的執行模式 , 8.
this lie group is a smooth , curved shape with 248 dimensions .	這個謊言團是一個抽菸、治癒了248度的形狀
each point in this pattern corresponds to a symmetry of this very complex and beautiful shape .	在這個模式中 , 在這個模式中 , 每一點非常複雜且美麗的形狀 。
one small part of this e8 shape can be used to describe the curved spacetime of einstein's general relativity , explaining gravity .	其中一小部分的形狀可以用來描述蛋白質的曲線 , 解釋了重力 , 解釋重力 。
together with quantum mechanics , the geometry of this shape could describe everything about how the universe works at the tiniest scales .	用量子機械 , 這種形狀可以描述宇宙如何運作 , 描述宇宙中最好的規模 。
the pattern of this shape living in eightdimensional charge space is exquisitely beautiful , and it summarizes thousands of possible interactions between these elementary particles , each of which is just a facet of this complicated shape .	這個形狀在八度空間中 , 生命的形狀很漂亮 , 它突然發現了數千種可能性粒子之間的互動 , 每一個元素之間的互動 。
as we spin it , we can see many of the other intricate patterns contained in this one .	隨著我們脊椎動物 , 我們可以看到許多其他特徵的模式 。
and with a particular rotation , we can look down through this pattern in eight dimensions along a symmetry axis and see all the particles at once .	有一種特殊的動作 , 我們可以在八度中觀察到這個模式中 , 看到所有粒子的粒子 , 看到所有粒子粒子 。
it's a very beautiful object , and as with any unification , we can see some holes where new particles are required by this pattern .	這是個非常漂亮的物體 , 我們能看到一些洞穴 , 新的粒子被這個模式所需要的洞見 。
there are 20 gaps where new particles should be , two of which have been filled by the patisalam particles .	有20個差距應該是新粒子 , 新粒子應該被填滿了粒子粒子 。
from their location in this pattern , we know that these new particles should be scalar fields like the higgs particle , but have color charge and interact with the strong force .	在這個模式中 , 我們知道這些新粒子應該是規模的 , 比如希格粒子粒子粒子粒子 , 但有顏色的力量 。
filling in these new particles completes this pattern , giving us the full e8 .	在這些新粒子裡 , 把我們整合起來 , 給我們整8 。
this e8 pattern has very deep mathematical roots .	這個時代有非常深的數學根源 。
it's considered by many to be the most beautiful structure in mathematics .	它被很多人認為是數學上最美麗的結構 。
it's a fantastic prospect that this object of great mathematical beauty could describe the truth of particle interactions at the smallest scales imaginable .	這是個很棒的數學證明 , 這個物體可以描述粒子互動的真相可以描述粒子之間最小的互動 。
and this idea that nature is described by mathematics is not at all new .	這個想法是 , 大自然是由數學描述出來的 。
in 1623 , galileo wrote this: " nature's grand book , which stands continually open to our gaze , is written in the language of mathematics .	在1623年 , 伽利略寫了: 「 大自然的書籍 , 站在數學上 , 不是數學的語言 。
its characters are triangles , circles and other geometrical figures , without which it is humanly impossible to understand a single word of it ; without these , one is wandering around in a dark labyrinth . "	它的角色是三角形 , 圓圈和其他幾何圖片 , 沒有它是不可能理解它的單一詞 ; 沒有這些 , 沒有人在黑暗實驗室裡 。 」
i believe this to be true , and i've tried to follow galileo's guidance in describing the mathematics of particle physics using only triangles , circles and other geometrical figures .	我相信這是真的 , 我試著遵循伽利略的數學指導 , 在描述數學中 , 只用三角形來描述數學數字 , 圓圈和其他幾何 。
of course , when other physicists and i actually work on this stuff , the mathematics can resemble a dark labyrinth .	當然 , 當我其他物理學家 , 我實際上在這個東西上工作時 , 數學可以重新組成一個黑暗實驗室 。
but it's reassuring that at the heart of this mathematics is pure , beautiful geometry .	但 , 在數學的心臟中 , 令人驚訝的是 , 美麗的幾何 , 美麗的遺跡 。
joined with quantum mechanics , this mathematics describes our universe as a growing e8 coral , with particles interacting at every location in all possible ways according to a beautiful pattern .	加入量子機械 , 這個數學描述我們宇宙的形式 , 以粒子描述我們宇宙的每一個可能性 , 粒子互相互動 。
and as more of the pattern comes into view using new machines like the large hadron collider , we may be able to see whether nature uses this e8 pattern or a different one .	隨著模式變得越來越多的新機器 , 比如大型的鐵路 , 我們可能可以看見大自然使用這個時代 , 或者不同的人 。
this process of discovery is a wonderful adventure to be involved in .	這種發現發現是一種很棒的冒險過程 。
if the lhc finds particles that fit this e8 pattern , that will be very , very cool .	如果lhc找到粒子的粒子 , 那就會非常酷 。
if the lhc finds new particles , but they don't fit this pattern well , that will be very interesting , but bad for this e8 theory .	如果lhc發現新粒子 , 但它們並不符合這個模式 , 那將會非常有趣 , 但對這個理論有趣 。
and , of course , bad for me personally .	當然 , 對我來說 , 對我來說 , 不好 。

well , pretty bad .	嗯 , 很糟 。

this theory and others like it are long shots .	這理論和其他像它很長的照片 。
one does a lot of hard work knowing that most of these ideas probably won't end up being true about nature .	第一 , 很多人都不知道這些想法大部分的想法可能是真的有關自然的 。

in this regard , new physics theories are a lot like startup companies .	在這個區域中 , 新物理學的理論很像開始創公司 。

now , the only way to maintain sanity and achieve happiness in the midst of this uncertainty is to keep balance and perspective in life .	現在 , 為了維持衛生和成幸福的唯一方法就是保持平衡和尊重生命的平衡 。
i've tried the best i can to live a balanced life .	我試過過最好的生命 。
i try to balance my life equally between physics , love and surfing my own three charge directions .	我試著平衡我的人生平等之間的平衡 , 愛和傷害我三位椅子的方向 。

that is the call that chimpanzees make before they go to sleep in the evening .	這就是黑猩猩的稱作黑猩猩在晚上睡覺 。
you hear it going from one side of the valley to the other , from one group of nests to the next .	你聽見它從谷歌到另一端 , 從其中一個群體到下一個群體之一 。
and i want to pick up with my talk this evening from where zeray left off yesterday .	我想拿著我的演講 , 昨天離開那晚上 。
he was talking about this amazing , threeyearold australopithecine child , selam .	他在談論這個很棒、三歲的童年 , 三歲的孩子 , 伊斯蘭 。
and we've also been hearing about the history , the family tree , of mankind through dna genetic profiling .	我們也聽到歷史、家人樹、家人樹、樹木、樹木、樹木、樹木、樹木、樹木 。
and it was a paleontologist , the late louis leakey , who actually set me on the path for studying chimpanzees .	這是一名古代學家 , 洛杉磯的洛杉磯 , 他真的在研究黑猩猩的路徑 。
and it was pretty extraordinary , way back then .	很不可思議 , 回到那之後 。
it's kind of commonplace now , but his argument was because he'd been searching for the fossilized remains of early humans in africa .	現在 , 這有點常見 , 但他的論點是因為他一直在尋找化石化化化石的早期 。
and you can tell an awful lot about what those beings looked like from the fossils , from the shape of the muscle attachments , something about the way they lived from the various artifacts found with them .	你可以告訴一個很糟糕的是那些被石油的形狀 , 從肌肉的形狀 , 從肌肉的形狀 , 關於它們生活的方式 , 關於它們生活的方式 。
but what about how they behaved ? that's what he wanted to know .	但他們到底怎麼樣呢 ? 這是他想要知道的 。
and of course , behavior doesn't fossilize .	當然 , 行為並不是化化石 。
he argued and it's now a fairly common theory that if we found behavior patterns similar or the same in our closest living relatives , the great apes , and humans today , then maybe those behaviors were present in the apelike , humanlike ancestor some seven million years ago .	他爭議了 , 正常常常常常常見的理論理論 , 如果我們發現行為模式相似或同 , 現今 , 偉大的寵物 , 也許這些行為都是在同儕、人類的行為 , 那麼 , 也許這些行為已經存在了七百萬年前的行為 。
and therefore , perhaps we had brought those characteristics with us from that ancient , ancient past .	因此 , 也許我們帶給這些特徵、古老、古老、古老的過去 。
well , if you look in textbooks today that deal with human evolution , you very often find people speculating about how early humans may have behaved , based on the behavior of chimpanzees .	嗯 , 如果你看看今天的書籍 , 你通常會發現人類演化的行為 , 你通常會發現人們在黑猩猩的行為行為 , 根據黑猩的行為行為行為行為行為行為行為的行為 。
they are more like us than any other living creature , and we've heard about that during this ted conference .	他們比其他生物其他生物生物更像我們在ted會議中聽到的 , 我們聽過這個ted會議 。
so it remains for me to comment on the ways in which chimpanzees are so like us , in certain aspects of their behavior .	所以 , 對我來說 , 黑猩猩來說 , 黑猩來說 , 黑猩的行為 , 就像我們一樣 , 在某些方面 ,
every chimpanzee has his or her own personality .	每隻黑猩猩有自己的個人性 。
of course , i gave them names . they can live to be 60 years or more , although we think most of them probably don't make it to 60 in the wild .	當然 , 我給他們名字
mr . wurzel . the female has her first baby when she's 11 or 12 .	mr.wurzel , 她的第一個嬰兒在11或12歲時 。
thereafter , she has one baby only every five or six years , a long period of childhood dependency when the child is nursing , sleeping with the mother at night , and riding on her back .	在五到六年 , 她有一個嬰兒只有每五到六歲的童年 , 一個長期的期期間 , 睡眠和母親一起睡 。
and we believe that this long period of childhood is important for chimpanzees , just as it is for us , in relation to learning .	我們相信這長期期期的童年很重要 , 就如黑猩猩的重要性 , 就像我們一樣 。
as the brain becomes ever more complex during evolution in different forms of animals , so we find that learning plays an ever more important role in an individual's life history .	當大腦變得更複雜 , 在演化過程中 , 我們發現學習玩耍更重要的角色 , 所以我們發現學習扮演了更重要的角色 。
and young chimpanzees spend a lot of time watching what their elders do .	年輕黑猩猩花了很多時間看他們的老闆 。
we know now that they're capable of imitating behaviors that they see .	我們現在知道他們有能力的行為 。
and we believe that it's in this way that the different toolusing behaviors that have now been seen in all the different chimpanzee populations studied in africa how these are passed from one generation to the next , through observation , imitation and practice , so that we can describe these toolusing behaviors as primitive culture .	我們相信這是不同的工具 , 在非洲各地不同的黑猩的行為 , 現在我們已經在非洲各地不同的黑猩研究 , 透過觀察到下一代 , 透過觀察和練習 , 通過觀察這些工具 , 我們可以描述這些工具 , 來描述這些工具 。
chimpanzees don't have a spoken language . we've talked about that .	黑猩猩沒有一隻蜘蛛語言 , 我們談過這一點 。
they do have a very rich repertoire of postures and gestures , many of which are similar , or even identical , to ours and formed in the same context . greeting chimpanzees embracing .	他們有一個非常豐富的重覆性 , 許多類似 , 甚至是相似的 , 甚至是相同的 , 甚至是同的 , 和我們的同情心 。
they also kiss , hold hands , pat one another on the back .	他們也技巧、手、手、手、握手 ,
and they swagger and they throw rocks .	而他們會把搖滾滾滾滾滾動 。
in chimpanzee society , we find many , many examples of compassion , precursors to love and true altruism .	在黑猩的社會中 , 我們發現很多很多同情心、受傷者、受傷者 , 來愛和真正的演變 。
unfortunately , they , like us , have a dark side to their nature .	不幸的是 , 他們就像我們一樣 , 有一個黑暗的面向 。
they're capable of extreme brutality , even a kind of primitive war .	他們有能力極度的戰爭 , 甚至有點驚人的戰爭 。
and these really aggressive behaviors , for the most part , are directed against individuals of the neighboring social group .	這些真的很有意見的行為 , 最重要的部分是對鄰居的社會團體 。
they are very territorially aggressive .	它們非常令人驚訝 。
chimpanzees , i believe , more than any other living creature , have helped us to understand that , after all , there is no sharp line between humans and the rest of the animal kingdom .	黑猩猩 , 我相信 , 比任何其他生物生物 , 幫助我們了解 , 畢竟 , 沒有鯊魚和其他動物之間的限制 。
it's a very blurry line , and it's getting more blurry all the time as we make even more observations .	這是個非常奇怪的線索 , 每當我們做更多的盲目 , 就像我們做更多的觀察 。
the study that i began in 1960 is still continuing to this day .	我在1960年開始一直持續持續持續持續持續 。
and these chimpanzees , living their complex social lives in the wild , have helped more than anything else to make us realize we are part of , and not separated from , the amazing animals with whom we share the planet .	而這些黑猩猩 , 牠們的複雜社會生活在野生動物身上 , 幫助我們了解到我們是一部分的 , 而不是從我們共享的動物 。
so it's pretty sad to find that chimpanzees , like so many other creatures around the world , are losing their habitats .	所以 , 很難找到黑猩猩 , 就像世界上許多其他生物一樣 , 都失去他們的棲息地 。
this is just one photograph from the air , and it shows you the forested highlands of gombe .	這只是從空氣中拍攝的照片 , 它給你看最高的目標之一 。
and it was when i flew over the whole area , about 16 years ago , and realized that outside the park , this forest , which in 1960 had stretched almost unbroken along the eastern shore of lake tanganyika , which is where the tiny , 30squaremile gombe national park lies , that a question came to my mind .	當我飛過整個區域時 , 大約16年前 , 我發現在公園裡 , 發現在公園裡 , 這種森林 , 在1960年代 , 幾乎沒有破壞了 , 那裡的海岸岸岸 , 三十公里 , 那是一個小型的國家公園 。
" how can we even try to save these famous chimpanzees , when the people living around the national park are struggling to survive ? "	「 我們怎麼能拯救這些有名黑猩猩 」 時 , 當我們住在國家公園裡的人會掙扎 ? "
more people are living there than the land could possibly support .	更多人居住在島嶼可以支持 。
the numbers increased by refugees pouring in from burundi and over the lake from congo .	數量的難民數量增加 , 從內部的湖泊和湖泊中湖泊的湖泊 。
and very poor people they couldn't afford to buy food from elsewhere .	非常窮人 , 他們無法負擔買食物 , 從其他地方買不到食物 。
this led to a program , which we call tacare .	這導致了一個計畫 , 我們稱之為 「 任務 」 。
it's a very holistic way of improving the lives of the people living in the villages around the park .	這是一個非常榮幸的方式來改善公園的生活方式 。
it started small with 12 villages . it's now in 24 .	它從24個村莊開始小村莊 , 現在在24歲 。
there isn't time to go into it , but it's including things like tree nurseries , methods of farming most suitable to this now very degraded , almost desertlike land up in these mountains .	沒有時間進入它 , 但它的影響 , 就像樹木護士一樣 , 包括農業、農業 , 幾乎是農業的 , 幾乎是農業的 。
ways of controlling , preventing soil erosion .	控制語言的方式 , 防止土壤 。
ways of reclaiming overused farmland , so that within two years they can again be productive .	重新思考農場的農場 , 兩年內 , 兩年內 , 可以再次生產力 。
working to help the villagers obtain fresh water from wells .	為了協助村民觀察者觀察者的水源 。
perhaps build some schoolrooms .	也許建造一些學校室 。
most important of all , i believe , is working with small groups of women , providing them with opportunities for microcredit loans .	最重要的是 , 我相信 , 就是和女性合作的小群體 , 提供他們機會 , 提供顯微的貸款 。
and we've got , as is the case around the world , about 95 percent of all loans returned .	我們得知 , 身為世界各地的案例 , 大約有95%的貸款 。
empowering women , working with education , providing scholarships for girls so they can finish secondary school , in the clear understanding that , all around the world , as women's education improves , family size drops .	賦予女性、教育、教育、教育、提供教育、教育、她們可以完成第二個學校 , 明顯地了解 , 所有世界各地的學校 , 都是女性的教育 。
we provide information about family planning and about hiv/aids .	我們提供關於家庭計劃和愛滋病的資訊 。
and as a result of this program , something's happening for conservation .	作為這個計畫的結果 , 有些東西正在發生 。
what's happening for conservation is that the farmers living in these 24 villages , instead of looking on us as a bunch of white people coming to study a whole bunch of monkeys and by the way , many of the staff are now tanzanian but when we began the tacare program , it was a tanzanian team going into the villages .	保育計畫是 , 農夫住在這24個村莊 , 而不是在尋找我們身為一群白人人人來研究一堆白人人人來研究一堆猴子 , 我們現在開始坦尚尼亞的團隊 , 但當我們開始塔利亞的塔利亞團隊 。
it was a tanzanian team talking to the villagers , asking what they were interested in .	這是一個坦尚尼亞團隊和村莊談談談他們對什麼興趣 。
were they interested in conservation ? absolutely not .	他們很感興趣嗎 ? 絕對不是 。
they were interested in health ; they were interested in education .	他們對健康有興趣 , 他們對教育有興趣 。
and as time went on , and as their situation began to improve , they began to understand ever more about the need for conservation .	隨著時間到來 , 當他們的情況開始改善 , 他們開始了解保育 , 他們開始了解更多關於保育需求的需求 。
they began to understand that as the upper levels of the hills were denuded of trees , so you've got this terrible soil erosion and mudslides .	他們開始了解 , 身為山頂層的頂層 , 所以你有了這可怕的土壤和mulidelideslideslideslideslides 。
today , we are developing what we call the greater gombe ecosystem .	今天 , 我們正在開發出我們稱之為 「 更好的目標 」 。
this is an area way outside the national park , stretching out into all these very degraded lands .	這是國家公園外公園 , 站在全國公園裡 , 站在這些島嶼上 。
and as these villages have a better standard of life , they are actually agreeing to put between 10 percent and 20 percent of their land in the highlands aside , so that once again , as the trees grow back , the chimpanzees will have leafy corridors through which they can travel to interact as they must for genetic viability with other remnant groups outside the national park .	身為這些村莊有更好的標準 , 他們實際上同意將近10%到20%到高島上 , 所以 , 一旦樹木長回來 , 黑猩會再次 , 黑猩猩猩會透過彼此交互作用來互動 。
so tacare is a success .	所以tacare是一個成功的成功 。
we're replicating it in other parts of africa , around other wilderness areas which are faced with extreme population pressure .	我們在非洲各地的其他部分 , 其他見證都在面對極端人口壓力中 。
the problems in africa , however , as we've been discussing for the whole of these first couple of days of ted , are major problems .	然而 , 在非洲 , 我們一直在討論這些第一幾天的ted , 是主要問題 。
there is a great deal of poverty .	貧窮的貧窮 。
and when you get large numbers of people living in land that is not that fertile , particularly when you cut down trees , and you leave the soil open to the wind for erosion , as desperate populations cut down more and more trees , so that they can try and grow food for themselves and their families , what's going to happen ? something's got to give .	當你在土地上得到大量的人們 , 尤其是在樹木時 , 特別是當你切割樹的時候 , 你就離開了土壤 , 使人口砍伐更多樹木 , 所以他們可以嘗試和更多樹木 , 所以他們可以嘗試和食物 , 他們的家人 , 該怎麼做 ?
and the other problems in not only africa , but the rest of the developing world and , indeed , everywhere what are we doing to our planet ?	而不是非洲其他問題 , 而是開發中國家的其他問題 , 而是在於開發中國家 , 我們該怎麼做 ?
you know , the famous scientist , e . o . wilson said that if every person on this planet attains the standard of living of the average european or american , we need three new planets .	你知道嗎 , 歐盟科學家 , 歐巴森說 , 如果每個人在這個星球的標準 , 我們需要三個新的星球的標準 。
today , they are saying four . but we don't have them . we've got one .	今天 , 他們說四歲 , 但我們沒有他們 。
and what's happened ? i mean , the question here is , here we are , arguably the most intelligent being that's ever walked planet earth , with this extraordinary brain , capable of the kind of technology that is so well illustrated by these ted conferences , and yet we're destroying the only home we have .	發生了什麼事呢 ? 我的意思是 , 問題是 , 我們是 , 阿富汗最聰明的大腦 , 和這個極端的大腦 , 可以用這種技術來吸引地球 , 但是我們已經摧毀了我們唯一的機會 。
the indigenous people around the world , before they made a major decision , used to sit around and ask themselves , " how does this decision affect our people seven generations ahead ? "	世界各地的人 , 在他們做了一個主要決策之前 , 要求自己坐下來 , 問自己: 「 這決定如何影響我們的七代人 ? 」
today , major decisions and i'm not particularly talking about africa here , but the developed world major decisions involving millions of dollars , and millions of people , are often based on , " how will this affect the next shareholders' meeting ? "	今天 , 主要決策 , 我不是特別談論非洲 , 而是開發了數百萬美元 , 而是開發了世界上數百萬人 , 而數百萬人 , 通常是基於: 「 接下來會如何影響下下下一步 ? 」
and these decisions affect africa .	這些決定影響非洲 。
as i began traveling around africa talking about the problems faced by chimpanzees and their vanishing forests , i realized more and more how so many of africa's problems could be laid at the door of previous colonial exploitation .	當我開始到非洲各地的談話時 , 我意識到更多的非洲和他們的優勢 , 我意識到更多的非洲問題 , 更多的非洲問題可能是多麼大 。
so i began traveling outside africa , talking in europe , talking in the united states , going to asia .	所以我開始到非洲 , 和歐洲談話 , 談到亞洲 , 談到亞洲 。
and everywhere there were these terrible problems .	任何地方都有這些可怕的問題 。
and you know the kind i'm talking about . i'm talking about pollution .	你知道我正在談論污染污染 。 我正在談論污染污染污染 。
the air that we breathe that often poisons us .	我們呼吸 , 通常我們呼吸的空氣 。
the earth is poisoning our foods .	地球正在污染我們的食物 。
the water water is perhaps one of the most crucial issues that we're going to face in this century and everywhere water is being polluted by agricultural , industrial and household chemicals that still are being sprayed around the world , seemingly with the inability to profit from past experience .	水是或許我們要面對這個世紀最關鍵的問題之一就是農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、和家 。
the mangroves are being cut down ; the effects of things like the tsunami get worse .	曼格魯斯已經被砍掉 ; 像海嘯變得更糟 。
we've talked about the soil erosion .	我們談到土壤的土壤 。
we have the reckless burning of fossil fuels along with other greenhouse gasses , so called , leading to climate change .	我們有難以置信石燃料燃料燃料燃料燃料 , 稱為氣候變遷 。
finally , all around the world , people have begun to believe that there is something going on very wrong with our climate .	最後 , 世界各地 , 人們必須相信 , 對於氣候的影響 。
all around the world climates are mixed up .	世界各地的氣候被混合在一起 。
and it's the poor people who are affected worse .	這是那些影響最糟糕的人 。
it's africa that already is affected .	非洲已經影響了 。
in many parts of subsaharan africa , the droughts are so much worse .	在許多撒哈拉非洲 , 乾旱帶來非常糟糕 。
and when the rain does come , it so often leads to flooding and added distress , and the cycle of poverty and hunger and disease .	當雨林發生時 , 通常會導致洪水 , 會導致貧窮和飢餓的循環 , 以及疾病的循環 。
and the numbers of people living in an area that the land cannot support , who are too poor to buy food , who can't move away because the whole land is degraded .	而住在一個島嶼裡的人數數數不支持 , 誰太窮了 , 因為整個土地被剝奪 , 因為整個土地被摧毀 。
and so you get desertification creeping , creeping , creeping as the last of the trees are cut down .	所以 , 你得到沙漠的危機 , 回應 , 評估樹木的最後一棵樹被砍掉 。
and this kind of thing is not just in africa . it's all over the world .	這類事情不只是在非洲各地 。
so it wasn't surprising to me that as i was traveling around the world i met so many young people who seemed to have lost hope .	所以這不是讓我驚訝的是 , 當我在世界各地旅行時 , 我遇到許多年輕人 , 似乎失去希望 。
we seem to have lost wisdom , the wisdom of the indigenous people .	我們似乎失去智慧、智慧、智慧、智慧的智慧 。
i asked a question . " why ? "	我問一個問題: 「 為什麼 ? 」
well , do you think there could be some kind of disconnect between this extraordinarily clever brain , the kind of brain that the ted technologies exemplify , and the human heart ? talking about it in the nonscientific term , in terms of love and compassion . is there some disconnect ?	嗯 , 你認為有某種分析的大腦之間有某種距離 , ted科技的大腦 , 像是ted技術擴展 , 而人類心臟呢 ? 談到它在愛和同情心中 , 談到愛和同情心 。
and these young people , when i talk to them , basically they were either depressed or apathetic , or bitter and angry . and they said more or less the same thing , " we feel this way because we feel you've compromised our future and there's nothing we can do about it . "	而這些年輕人 , 當我跟他們談話時 , 他們基本上是憂鬱或憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒 。 」
we have compromised their future .	我們有複雜的未來 。
i've got three little grandchildren , and every time i look at them and i think how we've harmed this beautiful planet since i was their age , i feel this desperation .	我有三個小孫子 , 每次我看著他們 , 我想我們如何害怕這些美麗的星球 , 因為我是他們的年齡 , 我感覺到這個美麗的星球 。
and that led to this program we call roots and shoots , which began right here in tanzania and has now spread to 97 countries around the world .	這個計畫讓我們稱之為根廷和拍攝的計畫 , 這開始在坦尚尼亞 , 現在全世界傳播到97個國家 。
it's symbolic . roots make a firm foundation .	它是物理的 。 根根根源製造一個奇怪的基礎 。
shoots seem tiny ; to reach the sun they can break through a brick wall .	拍攝似乎很小 ; 到太陽能牆壁 , 到太陽能牆壁 。
see the brick wall as all these problems we've inflicted on the planet , environmental and social . it's a message of hope .	看看我們地球上所有問題都在衝突上 , 環境和社交 。 這是一種希望的訊息 。
hundreds and thousands of young people around the world can break through and can make this a better world for all living things .	全世界有數百名年輕人 , 可以從世界各地創造出更好的世界 。
the most important message of roots and shoots: every single one of us makes a difference , every single day .	最重要的訊息和根根根源:每一天 , 我們都會做出差異 , 每天都會做出差別 。
we have a choice . every one of us in this room , we have a choice as to what kind of difference we want to make .	我們有一個選擇 。 每個人都有選擇 。 我們有選擇的差異 。
the very poor have no choice . it's up to us to change things so that the poor have choice as well .	窮人沒有選擇 。 它會讓我們改變窮人的選擇 。 所以 , 窮人有選擇 。
the roots and shoots groups all choose three projects .	根根部和槍擊團團團體都選了三項計畫 。
it depends on how old they are , and which country , whether they're in a city or rural , as to what kinds of projects .	它依賴他們多久 , 而國家 , 無論他們在城市或鄉村 , 無論他們在一個城市或鄉村 ,
but basically , we have programs now from preschool right through university , with more and more adults starting their own roots and shoots groups .	但基本上 , 我們現在從懷疑大學的程式設計 , 從準備開始 , 更多成年人開始 , 拍攝自己的根位置和拍攝的團隊 。
and every group chooses , between them , three different kinds of project to make this a better world , recognizing that all these different problems are interconnected and impinge on each other .	每組組組選項之間 , 三種不同的計畫 , 讓這個更好的世界變得更好 , 了解這些不同的問題都在互相連結 , 並在彼此之間 。
so one of their projects will be to help their own human community .	所以 , 他們的一項計畫會協助自己自己自己的社區 。
and then , if they're able , they may raise money to help communities in other parts of the world .	然後 , 如果他們能做到 , 他們可能會提升到世界上其他部分的社區 。
one of their projects will be to help animals not just wildlife , domestic animals as well .	他們的項目之一會幫助動物不僅僅是野生動物 。
and one of their projects will be to help the environment that we all share .	他們的項目之一會幫助我們分享的環境 。
and woven throughout all of this is a message of learning to live in peace and harmony within ourselves , in our families , in our communities , between nations , between cultures , between religions and between us and the natural world .	所有這一切都是學習和平靜的訊息 , 在我們自己的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭之間之間之間 , 與我們之間之間 , 與自然界之間之間之間 。
we need the natural world . we cannot go on destroying it at the rate we are .	我們需要自然的世界 , 我們不能去摧毀它 。
we not do have more than this one planet .	我們沒有比這個星球還要多 。
just picking one or two of the projects right here in africa that the roots and shoots groups are doing , one or two projects only in tanzania , in uganda , kenya , south africa , congobrazzaville , sierra leone , cameroon and other groups . and as i say , it's in 97 countries around the world .	只挑選一個計畫 , 在非洲的根部和槍擊團團團體正在做 , 一或兩個計畫只有在坦尚尼亞、南非、南非、南非、南非、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、獅子、南非 , 和其他國家 。
of course , they're planting trees . they're growing organic vegetables .	當然 , 他們正在培養樹 , 他們正在成長的有機蔬菜 。
they're working in the refugee camps , with chickens and selling the eggs for a little amount of money , or just using them to feed their families , and feeling a sense of pride and empowerment , because they're no longer helpless and depending on others with their vegetables and their chickens .	他們在難民營營中工作 , 用雞蛋和賣雞蛋 , 賣雞蛋的蛋 , 或用它們來餵食他們的家庭 , 感受到他們家人 , 因為他們不再有幫助和自己 。
it's being used in uganda to give some psychological help to exchild soldiers .	它被用在烏干達給一些心理幫助的士兵 。

but oh , they're also working on hiv/aids .	但喔 , 他們也在愛滋病/aididaid 。

and unwanted pregnancies and things like that , which young people listen to better from other youth , rather than adults .	不可思議的懷孕 , 那些年輕人傾聽的人 , 而非成人傾聽 , 而不是成人 。
hope . that's the question i get asked as i'm going around the world: " jane , you've seen so many terrible things , you've seen your chimpanzees decrease in number from about one million , at the turn of the century , to no more than 150 , 000 now , and the same with so many other animals .	希望 , 這是我在世界各地的一個問題: 「 珍 , 你看過很多可怕的事情 , 你看過你的黑猩猩數目 , 你看過你的黑猩數目 , 轉到一百萬個動物 。

it's inspiring . and it brings me to my last category of hope , and we've heard about this so much in the last two days: this indomitable human spirit . this determination of people , the resilience of the human spirit , so that people who you would think would be battered by poverty , or disease , or whatever , can pull themselves up out of it , sometimes with a helping hand , and take their part in society , and take their part in changing the world .	它鼓舞了我最後兩天 , 它帶我去了希望 , 在過去兩天中 , 我們聽過這個人的精神 , 這種決定人類精神的精神 。 這決定了人類精神精神的責任 , 所以你會認為會被貧窮的人 , 所以你會覺得蝙蝠被貧窮 , 有時你會覺得蝙蝠 。

and just a last word on that the young woman who's running this entire conference center , i met her today .	最後一個詞 , 在那位年輕女性跑步這整個職業中心 , 我今天遇見她 。

and it was very , very exciting for me to meet her and see just one example of how young people , when they are empowered , given the opportunity to take action , to make the world a better place , truly are our hope for tomorrow .	對我來說 , 對我來說 , 非常興奮 , 對她來說 , 當他們被賦予行動時 , 讓世界變得更好 , 讓世界變得更好 , 讓世界變得更好 。
artist dianna cohen shares some tough truths about plastic pollution in the ocean and in our lives and some thoughts on how to free ourselves from the plastic gyre .	藝術家們分享一些關於塑膠污染污染污染污染的事實 , 在我們的人生中 , 有些想法是如何自由的 。
consumerism , global issues , green , mission blue , oceans , plastic	消費者主義、全球議題、綠色、海洋、海洋、塑膠、塑膠、塑膠、塑膠 。
dianna cohen: tough truths about plastic pollution	狄安娜•安娜:很難真理的真相 。
i'm a visual artist , and i'm also one of the cofounders of the plastic pollution coalition .	我是一個視覺藝術家 , 我也是其中一個塑膠污染的核心之一 。
i've been working with plastic bags , which i cut up and sew back together as my primary material for my artwork for the last 20 years .	我和塑膠袋一起工作 , 我把塑膠袋放在過去二十年裡 , 把我當作藝術作品當作我為藝術作品的作品 。
i turn them into two and threedimensional pieces and sculptures and installations .	我把它們轉為兩、三維空間和雕塑和雕塑和雕像 。
upon working with the plastic , after about the first eight years , some of my work started to fissure and break down into smaller little bits of plastic .	和塑膠合作之後 , 大約八年後 , 有些我的工作開始融化 , 一些塑膠 。
and i thought , " great .	我心想: 「 很好 。 」
it's ephemeral just like us . "	它就像我們一樣 。 」
upon educating myself a little further about plastics , i actually realized this was a bad thing .	在教育中 , 我意識到 , 關於塑膠 , 我真的意識到這是一件壞事 。
it's a bad thing that plastic breaks down into smaller little bits , because it's always still plastic .	它是個壞事 , 塑膠分成較小的一點 , 因為它總是仍然是塑膠 。
and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們發現的是 , 在海洋環境環境中有很多 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	然後 , 在過去幾年裡 , 學到關於太平洋的禮物和greyrey 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	而我認為這是許多人的反應 , 我認為這是許多人第一個反應 , 就是 「 喔 ! 我的天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們必須走出去那裡 , 清理這個東西 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	所以 , 我實際上研發了一個建議 , 兩度的捕魚 , 兩度的魚類 , 一隻螃蟹 , 一隻螃蟹 , 一隻螃蟹 , 牠和一隻寒冷的機器 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	而我的意見是要走出gyreyreis的意識 , 開始從塑膠、開始挑選塑膠、冷藏的塑膠 , 可以把它當作材料當作建築物的材料 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始和研究的人談談到gyreyre , 研究塑膠問題 , 在海洋環境環境中 , 我發現 , 清潔它會是個非常小的飲料 , 每天我都得要回到世界各地各地 , 我需要回到世界各地的照片 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的圖片是:我們需要找到方法的方法 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要把單一的產物和可避免塑膠 , 每天都進入全球規模的海洋環境 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	所以 , 看看這一點 , 我也意識到我真的很憤怒 。
i wasn't just concerned about plastic that you're trying to imagine out in the middle of the pacific ocean of which i have learned there are now 11 gyres , potentially , of plastic in five major oceans in the world .	我不只是擔心塑膠海洋中間的塑膠 , 而是我學到的塑膠海洋中間有11個玻璃 , 可能在五個大海裡 , 可能是 , 塑膠在五個大海洋裡 。
it's not just that gyre of plastic that i'm concerned about it's the gyre of plastic in the supermarket .	不只是塑膠我所說的 , 我擔心它是超市塑膠的魅力 。
i'd go to the supermarket and all of my food is packaged in plastic .	我要去超市超市和所有的食物都包包裝 。
all of my beverages are packaged in plastic , even at the health food market .	我所有人都在塑膠市場上包裝 , 即使在健康市場市場上 。
i'm also concerned about the plastic in the refrigerator , and i'm concerned about the plastic and the toxins that leach from plastic into us and into our bodies .	我也關心了塑膠 , 在咖啡廳裡 , 我很擔心塑膠和毒素 , 我擔心塑膠和毒素 , 從塑膠到我們的身體中 。
so i came together with a group of other people who were all looking at this issue , and we created the plastic pollution coalition .	所以 , 我和一群人一起看這個議題 , 我們創造了塑膠污染煤炭 。
we have many initiatives that we're working on , but some of them are very basic .	我們有許多正面的正面 , 但有些是非常基本的 。
one is: if 80 to 90 percent of what we're finding in the ocean of the marine debris that we're finding in the ocean is plastic , then why don't we call it what it is .	第一:如果有80%到海洋的海洋圖片 , 我們發現我們在海洋中發現的海洋是塑膠 , 那麼為什麼我們不稱它為它為甚麼 。
recycling everybody kind of ends their books about being sustainable and greening with the idea of recycling .	回收所有他們的書籍 , 關於保持穩定和綠色的概念 。
you put something in a bin and you don't have to think about it again .	你把東西放進蛋白質放進蛋白質的東西放在一起 。
what is the reality of that ?	那到底是什麼 ?
in the united states , less than seven percent of our plastics are recycled .	在美國 , 超過70%的塑膠是回收的 。
and if you really look into it , particularly when it comes to plastic bottles , most of it is only downcycled , or incinerated , or shipped to china .	如果你真的去看它 , 特別是當它來塑膠瓶 , 大部分是最低的 , 或者是中國 。
it is downcycled and turned into lesser things , while a glass bottle can be a glass bottle again or can be used again a plastic bottle can never be a plastic bottle again .	它被循環 , 轉化成較少的瓶子 , 雖然玻璃瓶可以再再再一次一次再一次塑膠瓶 , 也可以再再一次塑膠瓶 。
so this is a big issue for us .	這是我們對我們來說最大的議題 。
another thing that we're looking at and asking people to think about is we've added a fourth r onto the front of the " reduce , reuse , recycle , " three r's , and that is refuse .	另一件事 , 我們正在看著人們去思考 , 就是我們在 「 紅色 」 的第四個r , 回收、回收、回收、回收、回收、回收 , 那就是難民 。
whenever possible , refuse singleuse and disposable plastics .	然而如果可能 , 拒絕單一的塑膠和可避免塑膠 。
alternatives exist ; some of them are very oldschool .	替代性存在 ; 有些人非常古老的選擇 。
i myself am now collecting these cool pyrex containers and using those instead of glad and tupperware containers to store food in .	我現在現在在收集這些酷兒的精神 , 用這些方式來儲存這些酷兒 , 而不是玻璃 , 而是要儲存食物 。
and i know that i am doing a service to myself and my family .	我知道 , 我在做一個服務 , 以及我的家人 。

i've been intrigued by this question of whether we could evolve or develop a sixth sense a sense that would give us seamless access and easy access to metainformation or information that may exist somewhere that may be relevant to help us make the right decision about whatever it is that we're coming across .	我一直被這個問題 , 無論我們是否能進化或開發一個六個感知 , 可以給我們一個六個感知 , 或資訊可能存在某些地方 , 可能存在某些地方可以幫助我們做出正確的決策 , 來協助我們做出正確的決定 。

and so my research group at the media lab has been developing a series of inventions to give us access to this information in a sort of easy way , without requiring that the user changes any of their behavior .	所以 , 我的研究團隊在媒體實驗室研發了一系列發明了一系列的資訊 , 不管是用簡單的方式來改變它們的行為 。

phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	phyllisrodrisz和ichaelwafi有一個強大的朋友出生於世界貿易中心被殺害了 , 2001年11月11日 , 2001年11月11日 , 2001年 , 2001年 , 2001年 , 2001年 , 伊斯蘭克斯蘭克斯蘭人和平 。
culture , global issues , politics	文化、全球議題、政治議題 。
9/11 healing: the mothers who found forgiveness , friendship	9/11的亨利:那些找到認知、友誼、友誼、友誼 。
phyllis rodriguez: we are here today because of the fact that we have what most people consider an unusual friendship .	幻想茲:我們今天這裡有大部分人認為我們有多人認為一個不尋常的友誼 。
and yet , it feels natural to us now .	然而 , 這感覺很自然地對我們來說很自然 。
i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我第一次知道我的兒子已經在世界貿易中心 , 2001年11月11日 。
we didn't know if he had perished yet until 36 hours later .	我們不知道他是否有被告知 , 直到36小時後 。
at the time , we knew that it was political .	在那時 , 我們知道它是政治的 。
we were afraid of what our country was going to do in the name of our son my husband , orlando , and i and our family .	我們被害怕我們的國家將會在我們的兒子的名字 , 或土地 , 我和我的家人 。
and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到它 , 當我看到它時 , 很糟糕的爆炸時 , 很糟糕的爆炸 , 真的 , 我們不幸 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾週後 , 當zaciamoussaui被注意到 , 六分之六的混亂 , 美國政府稱呼恐怖主義 , 美國政府稱之為死刑 , 如果保守 , 我的丈夫 , 我和丈夫 。
through that and through human rights groups , we were brought together with several other victims' families .	透過人類權利團體 , 我們和其他受害者一起合作 。
when i saw aicha in the media , coming over when her son was indicted , and i thought , " what a brave woman .	當我在媒體上看到阿根廷時 , 到她兒子時 , 我心想: 「 勇敢女人 」 的勇氣 。
someday i want to meet that woman when i'm stronger . "	有一天 , 我想要見到那個女人的時候 。 」
i was still in deep grief ; i knew i didn't have the strength .	我仍然在深悲傷 , 我知道我沒有力量 。
i knew i would find her someday , or we would find each other .	我知道 , 我會找到她的日子 , 或者我們會找到彼此 。
because , when people heard that my son was a victim , i got immediate sympathy .	因為當人們聽到我兒子是個受害者 , 我得到立刻的對象 。
but when people learned what her son was accused of , she didn't get that sympathy .	但當人們知道她的兒子是被控訴 , 她沒有得到那樣的對象 。
but her suffering is equal to mine .	但她的苦難是平等的 。
so we met in november 2002 , and aicha will now tell you how that came about .	所以我們在2002年11月2日 , 阿根廷會告訴各位 , 這是怎麼回事 。
aicha elwafi: good afternoon , ladies and gentlemen .	aichaelwafi:好後午、女士、女士、女士 。
i am the mother of zacarias moussaoui .	我是阿拉伯的母親媽媽媽媽媽媽 。

i suffered a lot as a mother .	我受苦了很多母親 。
i was married when i was 14 .	當我14歲的時候 , 我結婚了 。
i lost a child when i was 15 , a second child when i was 16 .	當我十五歲時 , 我失去了一個孩子時 , 第二個孩子 。
so the story with zacarias was too much really .	所以 , 和薩薩薩薩薩拉的故事太多 。
and i still suffer , because my son is like he's buried alive .	我仍然受苦 , 因為我的兒子就像他被埋葬了 。

but she knows where he is .	但她知道他在哪裡 。
my son , i don't know where he is .	我的兒子 , 我不知道他在哪裡 。
i don't know if he's alive . i don't know if he's tortured .	我不知道他是否活著 , 我不知道他是否活著 。
i don't know what happened to him .	我不知道他發生什麼事 。
so that's why i decided to tell my story , so that my suffering is something positive for other women .	這就是為什麼我決定要告訴我的故事 , 所以我的苦惱是正面的 。
for all the women , all the mothers that give life , you can give back , you can change .	對所有婦女來說 , 所有的母親 , 你可以回復 , 你可以回復 。
it's up to us women , because we are women , because we love our children .	對我們來說 , 女人來說 , 因為我們很愛我們的孩子 。
we must be handinhand and do something together .	我們必須有手臂 , 一起做些什麼事 。
it's not against women , it's for us , for us women , for our children .	這不是對女性來說 , 對我們來說 , 對我們來說 , 對我們的孩子來說 , 對我們的孩子來說 ,
i talk against violence , against terrorism .	我對抗暴力 , 反抗恐怖主義 。
i go to schools to talk to young , muslim girls so they don't accept to be married against their will very young .	我去上學到年輕、穆斯林女孩 , 所以穆斯林女孩們 , 他們不接受他們 ,

this is why i'm here in front of you .	這就是為什麼我在你們面前 。
pr: i would like to say that i have learned so much from aicha , starting with that day we had our very first meeting with other family members which was a very private meeting with security , because it was november 2002 , and , frankly , we were afraid of the superpatriotism of that time in the country those of us family members .	pr:我想說 , 我學到了很多來自阿根廷 , 從那天開始 , 我們和其他家庭成員 , 這是非常私人的成員 , 因為這不是2002年11月2002日 , 坦白說 , 我們是害怕的超級恐怖主義 。
but we were all so nervous .	但我們都很緊張 。
" why does she want to meet us ? "	「 為什麼她想要見我們 ? 」
and then she was nervous .	然後她很緊張 。
" why did we want to meet her ? "	「 為什麼我們想見她 ? 」

then we sat in a circle with support , with help , from people experienced in this kind of reconciliation .	然後我們坐在一個圓圈裡 , 協助來自這種連結 , 從人體體體驗中的人體驗 。
and aicha started , and she said , " i don't know if my son is guilty or innocent , but i want to tell you how sorry i am for what happened to your families .	阿根廷開始 , 她說: 「 我不知道我的兒子是罪惡或無辜 , 但我想要告訴各位 , 我是如何對你的家庭有多抱歉 。
i know what it is to suffer , and i feel that if there is a crime , a person should be tried fairly and punished . "	我知道它是如何苦難 , 我覺得如果有犯罪 , 一個人應該被審判和懲罰 。 」
but she reached out to us in that way , and it was , i'd like to say , it was an icebreaker .	但她伸出去 , 我想要說 , 那是個冰淇淋 , 我想說 , 那是個冰淇淋 。

before lifesaver , the best hand filters were only capable of filtering down to about 200 nanometers .	在生命sa版本之前 , 最好的手濾器只能在200000英尺 。

lifesaver pores are 15 nanometers .	生命版本是15奈米粒子 。
so nothing is getting through .	所以 , 什麼都沒有經歷過 。

paddy ashdown claims that we are living in a moment in history where power is changing in ways it never has before . in a spellbinding talk at tedxbrussels he outlines the three major global shifts that he sees coming .	幸運的是 , 我們在歷史上生活的時刻 , 力量正在改變它從未有過的時刻 , 在tedxbrusel的演講中 , 他在tedxbrusel , 他看到了三個主要全球轉變 。

paddy ashdown: the global power shift	幸運的是 , 全球權力轉變 。
there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在19世紀末末 , 有一首詩的英文詩 , 在19世紀末末 ,
it was said to echo in churchill's brain in the 1930s .	那是193030年代的腦袋裡 。
and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die . "	詩人說: 「 在夏天 , 我和夏天的流動 , 笑著我聽到一個奇怪的飲料 , 像是夢裡的聲音 , 我聽到一個遙遠的飲食 , 到地球上 。 」
those who are interested in poetry , the poem is " a shropshire lad " written by a . e . housman .	詩人對詩人感到興趣 , 詩是 「 商店 」 寫著 「 店 」 寫作 」 寫作 。
but what housman understood , and you hear it in the symphonies of nielsen too , was that the long , hot , silvan summers of stability of the 19th century were coming to a close , and that we were about to move into one of those terrifying periods of history when power changes .	但霍爾曼了解到 , 你也聽到它 , 在尼爾的象徵中聽到它 , 長期、熱情、熱情、熱情、熱情、熱情的夏天 , 我們要搬進過去的一步 , 我們要搬到歷史中 , 當我們改變歷史的力量 。
and these are always periods , ladies and gentlemen , accompanied by turbulence , and all too often by blood .	這些都是永久的、女士、女士、女士、女士、女士 , 都被血液 。
and my message for you is that i believe we are condemned , if you like , to live at just one of those moments in history when the gimbals upon which the established order of power is beginning to change and the new look of the world , the new powers that exist in the world , are beginning to take form .	我的訊息是 , 我相信我們是擔心的 , 如果你喜歡 , 在歷史上 , 只要你活在歷史上最高的力量之一之一 , 就能改變世界 , 世界的新勢力是開始改變 , 世界的新勢力是開始的 。
and these are and we see it very clearly today nearly always highly turbulent times , highly difficult times , and all too often very bloody times .	這些都是今天我們看到的 , 很顯然 , 幾乎總是很高 , 而且常常常常常很血腥 。
by the way , it happens about once every century .	順便一提 , 每世紀都發生了 。
you might argue that the last time it happened and that's what housman felt coming and what churchill felt too was that when power passed from the old nations , the old powers of europe , across the atlantic to the new emerging power of the united states of america the beginning of the american century .	你可能會說 , 最後一次它發生了 , 那就是華盛頓的感受 , 以及教堂的感受 , 當歐洲從古老的國家開始 , 到歐洲 , 在大西洋的新興力量 , 橫跨美國世紀初期的力量 。
and of course , into the vacuum where the tooold european powers used to be were played the two bloody catastrophes of the last century the one in the first part and the one in the second part: the two great world wars .	當然 , 在過去的世紀中 , 歐洲權力已經扮演了兩個血管 , 首先 , 在過去一世紀初 , 第二部份是:兩個偉大的戰爭 。
mao zedong used to refer to them as the european civil wars , and it's probably a more accurate way of describing them .	馬羅曾經曾經被迫害到歐洲民戰鬥 , 可能更加準確的方式 , 可能更準確的方式描述他們 。
well , ladies and gentlemen , we live at one of those times .	嗯 , 女士們 , 我們住在這些時候 。
but for us , i want to talk about three factors today .	但對我們來說 , 我想談三個因素 。
and the first of these , the first two of these , is about a shift in power .	首先 , 這些都是關於權力的轉變 。
and the second is about some new dimension which i want to refer to , which has never quite happened in the way it's happening now .	第二個是關於一些新的方向 , 我想重新設計師 , 這從來沒有發生過的事 。
but let's talk about the shifts of power that are occurring to the world .	但我們來談談這個權力改變世界的改變 。
and what is happening today is , in one sense , frightening because it's never happened before .	今天發生的是 , 在某種意義上 , 因為它從未發生過的事 。
we have seen lateral shifts of power the power of greece passed to rome and the power shifts that occurred during the european civilizations but we are seeing something slightly different .	後來我們看到希臘的力量轉變為羅馬和權力轉移到羅馬和權力轉變 , 但我們看到了一些事情 。
for power is not just moving laterally from nation to nation .	權力不只是從國家搬到國家 。
it's also moving vertically .	它也在移動了版本 。
what's happening today is that the power that was encased , held to accountability , held to the rule of law , within the institution of the nation state has now migrated in very large measure onto the global stage .	今天發生的是 , 國內的力量 , 他告訴了法律 , 他告訴了法律 , 在美國國家的規則中 , 在非常大的測量 , 在全球階段中 , 非常大的測量 。
the globalization of power we talk about the globalization of markets , but actually it's the globalization of real power .	我們談到市場的全球化化化 , 但事實上它是真實力量的全球化化化 。
and where , at the nation state level that power is held to accountability subject to the rule of law , on the international stage it is not .	在那裡 , 在國際階段中 , 權力是他要求法律 , 在國際階段 , 不是 。
the international stage and the global stage where power now resides: the power of the internet , the power of the satellite broadcasters , the power of the money changers this vast moneygoround that circulates now 32 times the amount of money necessary for the trade it's supposed to be there to finance the money changers , if you like , the financial speculators that have brought us all to our knees quite recently , the power of the multinational corporations now developing budgets often bigger than mediumsized countries .	國際舞台和全球舞台的力量:現在網際網路的力量 , 衛星的力量力量 , 金錢改變了這個巨大的金錢改變了這個巨大的金錢 , 將錢轉換為貿易的貿易金錢轉換為我們所需的金錢 , 將錢轉換為我們所帶來的財務 , 例如 , 如果你的財政部門 。
these live in a global space which is largely unregulated , not subject to the rule of law , and in which people may act free of constraint .	這些生活在一個全球空間中 , 不管是法律的規則 , 而在那些人可能自由的規則 。
now that suits the powerful up to a moment .	現在 , 突然間有強大的力量 。
it's always suitable for those who have the most power to operate in spaces without constraint , but the lesson of history is that , sooner or later , unregulated space space not subject to the rule of law becomes populated , not just by the things you wanted international trade , the internet , etc . but also by the things you don't want international criminality , international terrorism .	總之總是永續發展最有權力的人 , 沒有矛盾 , 但歷史歷史的教訓就是這樣 , 不久 , 不久 , 不管是法律的 , 不是你想要國際貿易、網際貿易、網際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、非政府主義 。
the revelation of 9/11 is that even if you are the most powerful nation on earth , nevertheless , those who inhabit that space can attack you even in your most iconic of cities one bright september morning .	911事件是 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 除非 , 除非 , 那些在你大部分城市中最強大的城市之一 。
it's said that something like 60 percent of the four million dollars that was taken to fund 9/11 actually passed through the institutions of the twin towers which 9/11 destroyed .	它說 , 大約有60%的錢是為了募款9/11 , 其實是從塔塔塔到鎮鎮鎮上 , 911事件被摧毀了 。
you see , our enemies also use this space the space of mass travel , the internet , satellite broadcasters to be able to get around their poison , which is about destroying our systems and our ways .	你知道嗎 , 我們的敵人也使用這個空間 , 網路、網路、衛星、衛星、衛星、衛星、衛星和我們的方式 。
sooner or later , sooner or later , the rule of history is that where power goes governance must follow .	很快 , 不久後 , 歷史的規則是 , 權力的規則必須遵循 。
and if it is therefore the case , as i believe it is , that one of the phenomenon of our time is the globalization of power , then it follows that one of the challenges of our time is to bring governance to the global space .	如果這是我相信這個案例 , 就像我相信這是我們時代的一個現象之一的全球化 , 然後它遵循我們時間的挑戰之一 , 然後它遵循全球空間的挑戰之一 。
and i believe that the decades ahead of us now will be to a greater or lesser extent turbulent the more or less we are able to achieve that aim: to bring governance to the global space .	我相信 , 十年來 , 我們現在將會成為更大 , 或更少的外星人 , 才能達到這個目標:帶領目標:把目標轉換到全球空間 。
now notice , i'm not talking about government .	現在注意到 , 我不是在談論政府 。
i'm not talking about setting up some global democratic institution .	我不是要談設定一些全球民主機構 。
my own view , by the way , ladies and gentlemen , is that this is unlikely to be done by spawning more u . n . institutions .	我自己的觀點來看 , 女士們們 , 就是這真的很不可思議地做過更多u.機構 。

it needs a means by which you can legitimize international action .	它需要一個意思是 , 你可以合法化國際行動 。
but when it comes to governance of the global space , my guess is this won't happen through the creation of more u . n . institutions .	但當它來到全球空間時 , 我的猜測是這不是透過創造更多美國的創意 。
it will actually happen by the powerful coming together and making treatybased systems , treatybased agreements , to govern that global space .	實際上 , 它會是由強大的組成 , 以治療基礎設施 , 將全球空間轉化為基礎 。
and if you look , you can see them happening , already beginning to emerge .	如果你看 , 你可以看到他們正在發生 , 已經開始擁抱 。
the world trade organization: treatybased organization , entirely treatybased , and yet , powerful enough to hold even the most powerful , the united states , to account if necessary .	世界貿易組織:治療y基礎組織 , 完全對待最強大 , 但強大到美國 , 如果必要的必要 。

now there's a problem there , and we'll come back to it in a minute , which is that if you bring the most powerful together to make the rules in treatybased institutions , to fill that governance space , then what happens to the weak who are left out ?	現在有一個問題 , 我們會回到它 , 在一分鐘內 , 如果你把最強大的機構結合在一起 , 那就就是 , 以治療基礎設施的規則 , 來填補這些弱點 , 那麼弱點會發生什麼事 ?

so there's my first message , that if you are to pass through these turbulent times more or less turbulently , then our success in doing that will in large measure depend on our capacity to bring sensible governance to the global space .	所以 , 我的第一個訊息是 , 如果你通過這些外科手術時 , 我們的成功率更少 , 然後我們的成功 , 我們的成功 , 將成功地放在全球空間中 , 將成功地帶到全球空間中 。
and watch that beginning to happen .	看看那一開始發生 。
my second point is , and i know i don't have to talk to an audience like this about such a thing , but power is not just shifting vertically , it's also shifting horizontally .	我的第二點是 , 我知道我不需要跟像這樣的觀眾談話 , 但權力不只是轉變版版版本 。
you might argue that the story , the history of civilizations , has been civilizations gathered around seas with the first ones around the mediterranean , the more recent ones in the ascendents of western power around the atlantic .	你可能會說故事 , 文明歷史文明的歷史歷史 , 一直在文明中 , 有文明的第一件事 , 在西方的西方國家 , 越是西洋棋的 。

my guess is , for what it's worth , is that the united states will remain the most powerful nation on earth for the next 10 years , 15 , but the context in which she holds her power has now radically altered ; it has radically changed .	我的猜測是 , 對美國而言 , 美國將會維持最強大的國家將會維持最強大的國家 , 但她在未來十年內 , 15年 , 她把她的權力已經改變了 。
we are coming out of 50 years , most unusual years , of history in which we have had a totally monopolar world , in which every compass needle for or against has to be referenced by its position to washington a world bestrode by a single colossus .	我們從五十年來 , 大部分的歷史中 , 歷史上我們必須完全現代的歷史 , 無論是對華盛頓世界最好的 , 無論是華盛頓世界最好的 。

now notice , in a period which is dominated by a monopolar world , you have fixed alliances nato , the warsaw pact .	注意到 , 在一個永久的世界中 , 被一個月球的世界中 , 你有固定的所有技巧 , 戰爭sawpt 。

canning , the great british foreign secretary once said , " britain has a common interest , but no common allies . "	可以否否認 , 偉大英國安全局說: 「 英國有共同點 , 但沒有共同點 。 」

today in our modern world , because of the internet , because of the kinds of things people have been talking about here , everything is connected to everything .	今天在我們的現代世界 , 因為網際網路 , 人們一直在談論這件事 , 一切都連結到一切 。

and what that means is the idea of a nation state acting alone , not connected with others , not working with others , is no longer a viable proposition .	這意味著 , 國家行動獨自行動的概念 , 不是與其他人合作 , 而不是與其他人合作 , 而是不再是可靠的 。
because the actions of a nation state are neither confined to itself , nor is it sufficient for the nation state itself to control its own territory , because the effects outside the nation state are now beginning to affect what happens inside them .	因為一個國家的行動行為行為 , 不管是自己對國家來說 , 沒有效率 , 沒有效率 , 因為國家本身的效果 , 現在就開始影響自己的恐怖狀態 。
i was a young soldier in the last of the small empire wars of britain .	我是一位年輕士兵在英國最小的帝國戰爭中 。

it's no longer the case that the security of a country is simply a matter for its soldiers and its ministry of defense .	它不再是國家安全的安全狀況 , 只是為了它士兵的安全 , 且它的礦坑 , 它的礦坑 。

you in business know that the paradigm structure of our time , ladies and gentlemen , is the network .	在我們的時間中 , 女士們知道 , 女士、女士、女士、網絡 。
